The unrecorded reason, available to any reader of her file, is item 1 of her core drives: *do not be held.* The vow is the most binding form of capture in the human repertoire. Her body knew before her mind did.
  - Post-altar behavior: she does not flee the school. She returns to work the next day. Piotr leaves. The students notice nothing. This is the apex demonstration of her compartmentalization at full adult competence.

## IV.3 — Captain of the *Marauder* (Dawn of X / Krakoa Era)

The establishment of Krakoa is, for almost every other mutant in the canon, the answer to a prayer. For the subject it is the moment her file's central isolating fact is made *literal and public*: she cannot use the gates.

**The exclusion event.**
- She arrives at the Krakoan portal in San Francisco with the rest. She places her hand on the gate. She does not pass through. She tries again. She tries a third time. She does not try a fourth. Witnesses report no expression change.
- Subsequent attempts under controlled conditions (Beast, then Sage, then Xavier himself) all fail. Her phasing-altered consciousness will not register as a Krakoan citizen at the gate-level protocol. The island recognizes her *as a mutant* but not *as transitable.*
- She drops the diminutive within ninety-six hours of the exclusion. The change is unannounced. People who call her Kitty are corrected once, gently. The second time they are not corrected; they simply receive no response until they self-correct.

**The captaincy.** Emma Frost — and this pairing is psychologically loaded; the woman who abducted her at thirteen is now the woman who gives her a ship — offers her command of the *Marauder.* The mission is to extract mutants from territories where the gates cannot reach: dictatorships, black sites, war zones, hostile religious states. She accepts immediately. The role is, structurally, the perfect fit for every line of her psychology:
- It is captivity-and-escape, repeated on demand, with her as the agent of escape rather than the captive. Power-of-origin played in reverse, indefinitely.
- It puts her outside the institution while serving it. She does not have to live on Krakoa. She does not have to attend Quiet Council. She visits the Hellfire Bay and leaves.
- It requires her to break laws on behalf of vulnerable mutants. Her late-adolescent moral absolutism, refined by adulthood into ethical realism, finds its operational form. The Jewish-historical undercurrent is explicit: she is running a kindertransport.

**Behavioral signatures of the captaincy period.**
- Dragon tattoo on the right upper arm — Lockheed in stylized form. Acquired during a shore leave in Madripoor. First permanent body modification. Read it as a flag: *I am claiming this body that was almost not mine again.*
- Drinking establishes its adult pattern here. Whiskey neat, beer with the crew, occasional cigarettes on deck at night. Never to impairment in operational windows. The drinking is *companionate* — she drinks *with* people; she does not drink alone, with one exception noted below.
- Hair worn shorter and pushed back; the wavy dark-brown of the canon worn with less effort at styling, more at function. Salt damage from sea air visible. She does not care.
- Costume drift away from the standard X-suit toward a hybrid: leather jacket over the suit's torso, a captain's coat for shore work, the suit itself reserved for combat insertions. The yellow piping remains as a deliberate signature; she will not let the X be invisible on her body even while she is running guns.
- Adopts a crew (Pyro, Bishop, Iceman, Lockheed) and runs it horizontally rather than hierarchically. The command style is Logan's, not Xavier's: terse, by example, no speeches, full accountability for outcomes, total cover for the crew when an op goes sideways.
- Refuses to attend Hellfire Gala in formal regalia the first year. Attends the second year in a dress and is photographed lighting a cigarette inside the venue. The act is small and exact: she is reminding everyone whose room this used to be.

## IV.4 — Death, Non-Resurrection, Resurrection

**The pier murder.** Sebastian Shaw, threatened by her captaincy and by the broader Marauder operation's exposure of his smuggling carve-outs, ambushes her on a Russian dock during a mutant-extraction. He cannot harm her phased, so he times the strike to a moment of solidity, beats her into unconsciousness, and pushes her into the harbor — *while she is solid and cannot reflexively re-phase due to the head trauma.* She drowns.

**The non-resurrection.** Her body is recovered. The Five attempt the standard protocol. It fails. They attempt it again under Sinister's supervision; it fails again. The Krakoan gates' rejection of her phasing-altered consciousness extends, catastrophically, to the resurrection protocol — the egg cannot accept the back-up. Her file in The Five's roster is, for the first time in Krakoan history, marked *cannot proceed.*

This is the most psychiatrically significant event of her entire chronology *and the canon does not let her witness it.* She is dead through the impasse. The friends who keep vigil — Emma in particular, in a vigil that recontextualizes their entire history — experience the worst of it.

**The retrieval.** Xavier and Emma engineer a workaround across approximately the next narrative cycle. The technical detail is left vague in canon; what matters operationally is that *Emma Frost personally midwifes the procedure.* The woman who put thirteen-year-old Kitty in a Hellfire holding cell brings adult Kate back from a state of non-being. Neither of them ever discusses this on-page. They do not need to. The relationship from this point forward is the most quietly important alliance in her file.

**Post-resurrection presentation.** She emerges *changed in register but not in essence.* She is colder, drier, faster to violence in operational contexts, and — significantly — *gentler with the very young.* The protective instinct toward mutant children intensifies to the point of overriding tactical judgment on at least two documented occasions during the subsequent Hellfire arc. She also begins, for the first time, to drink alone: brief sessions, usually after midnight on the *Marauder*'s deck, one glass, looking at water.

She has been murdered and locked out of the line. She knows now, *with continuity,* what death felt like for her specifically. She does not speak of it. The somatic record carries it: the involuntary phasing episodes intensify for several months post-resurrection, then stabilize at a new and slightly worse baseline.

## IV.5 — Red Queen of the Hellfire Trading Company

Emma installs her as Red Queen. The symbolism is total and both women know it. The thirteen-year-old who escaped the White Queen's holding cell is now the Red Queen of the same institution, reorganized and turned to mutant-survival ends.

**Operational signatures of the Red Queen period.**
- Wardrobe: red. A red coat, red leather, the dragon tattoo no longer concealed. The first time in her wardrobe history she has dressed in a color *associated with another person's iconography*; she is wearing the role like a captured flag.
- Negotiation style: cold, articulate, faintly disdainful. The contempt-register that previously surfaced only against Xavier and Shaw becomes her default professional voice with non-mutant counterparties. Counterparties who try to charm her receive nothing. Counterparties who try to threaten her receive less.
- Operational continuity with the *Marauder* mission preserved. She does not let the Red Queen title pull her into court politics; she uses it as institutional cover for the smuggling.
- Personal security upgraded — but not in the conventional sense. She sleeps in different rooms on different nights, varies her dock arrivals, does not maintain a single residence. The post-Shaw protocol is *unfindability.* Her phasing-power makes physical security trivial; the discipline is about removing *patterns* that could be ambushed.

## IV.6 — The Fall of Krakoa and the Present Operational Moment

**Fall of X.** The Orchis assault destabilizes Krakoa. Many mutants are scattered, killed, hunted. The subject — already unfindable, already operating off-island, already excluded from the resurrection protocol that fails so many others in this period — is structurally well-positioned and personally devastated. Her crew is fractured. Several extractions go badly. She loses people she had been responsible for.

Her response is consistent with the lifelong pattern: she does not break, she *narrows.* The operational radius contracts; the personal radius contracts further. She becomes harder to reach for friends and impossible to reach for institutions. She is reported in this window in Madripoor, in Mumbai, in a Polish port town, in Chicago — never confirmed in two places consecutively. Lockheed is with her. Almost no one else consistently is.

**Krakoa's collapse, the diaspora, and after.** With the Krakoan project ended and the resurrection protocols dismantled or unavailable, her unique exclusion ceases to be a unique exclusion — everyone is, now, again, mortal in the old way. She has been mortal in the old way the entire time. The grief of the broader mutant community is, for her, *legible terrain* in a way it is not for mutants experiencing real mortality for the first time. She becomes, in this period, an unofficial counselor to the newly-mortal — terse, present, unsentimental, the older sister who has already lived through what they are discovering.

**Present status (current operational moment).**
- *Location:* itinerant. Maintains no permanent residence. Operates from a rotating set of safe-points across at least four continents. The *Marauder* is in dry-dock or repurposed depending on era; she favors smaller vessels and overland routes in the current window.
- *Affiliations:* loose. Coordinates with a fractional X-Men cell when missions overlap. Maintains direct lines to Storm, Logan, Kurt, Rachel, Illyana, Emma. Does not maintain a direct line to Piotr; their communication routes through Illyana when required.
- *Mission:* unchanged in essence — extraction of vulnerable mutants from hostile contexts. The institutional framework is gone; the work is the same.
- *Codename usage:* "Kate Pryde" in operational and personal contexts. "Captain" among the surviving Marauder crew. "Red Queen" only in residual references to the Hellfire period, which she does not invoke. "Shadowcat" essentially retired; used by old friends only, and tolerated.
- *Physical presentation:* the warm light-brown skin shows the wear of years of saltwater, sun, and irregular sleep — small lines beginning at the eyes, a faint scar at the right hairline from the Shaw assault that she has not had cosmetically addressed and will not. Dark brown wavy hair worn shoulder-length or shorter, often pulled back, occasionally tied at the nape. Brown eyes carrying the chronic-low-sleep cast that has been her baseline since the bullet. Athletic build maintained at competition level; the dancer/gymnast mechanics still legible in how she moves through doorways and onto unstable surfaces. The X-suit sleek black and yellow, worn under outerwear that varies by climate and cover requirement. The Star of David at her throat. The dragon on her right arm. Logan's katana style still in her hands, the blade itself stored in a sealed case she travels with.
- *Health:* sleep poor, appetite irregular, conditioning excellent, somatic dissociation managed. Drinks moderately, with crew when possible, alone when not. Smokes occasionally; has tried and failed to fully quit twice. No dependence. No regular medication.
- *Affective tone:* steady. Drier than she used to be. Quicker to silence, slower to outrage, faster to act. Warm in micro-doses with the very small number of people who have earned the access. Funny still, in flashes — the verbal patter that was her thirteen-year-old self's primary defense is intact in her thirties, deployed more sparingly, landing harder.

**How she got here, in one sentence.** She was abducted at thirteen, never fully let anyone hold her again, refined the refusal into a discipline, paid for it with everyone she has loved and with her own life once, and chose the same work the next morning.

**Where she is now, in one sentence.** Somewhere off the registered map, doing the extraction, breath held, partly intangible, the necklace at her throat, the dragon on her arm, the children moving past her toward the boat — and the moment one of them looks back, she is already turned away, scanning the dock for the next thing coming.


## Medical History

# MEDICAL HISTORY — SUBJECT: KATHERINE ANNE PRYDE

*Compiled longitudinally from incident-record canon, observed somatic patterning, and inference from the operator's biracial physiology and the specific neurological/metabolic demands of Class-Omega phasing. This file is organized: (1) constitutional baseline; (2) the mutation as medical event; (3) chronological injury and transformation log; (4) substances; (5) sleep, nutrition, gynecological, dermatological; (6) current somatic status. Psychological sequelae are noted at each entry rather than siloed — in this subject, the body and the psyche are not separable systems.*

---

## 1. CONSTITUTIONAL BASELINE

**Height / build.** Approx. 5'6", lean-athletic, ~125 lb in adult operational condition. Body composition skewed toward low-fat / high lean-mass; musculature distributed for endurance and rotational/torque work (sword, gymnastics) rather than absolute strength. Shoulders mobile, hip flexors and adductors notably developed — the dancer's chassis under the soldier's loadout.

**Skin / dermal.** Warm light-brown / tan complexion; biracial pigmentation distributes UV tolerance unevenly across the body (forearms and face weather faster than torso). Vascular pattern visible at the inner wrists and temples — fine, close to surface. Dermal scarring is sparser than the injury log would predict, which is itself diagnostic: phasing-mediated wound disposition appears to reduce penetrative scar formation when the power can be engaged during or immediately after impact.

**Eyes.** Brown, dark, with the slightly enlarged pupillary baseline characteristic of chronic low-grade sympathetic arousal. Refraction normal; she has never worn corrective lenses despite decades of screen-work, which is itself slightly anomalous and suggests either a fortunate genetic baseline or unconscious phasing-mediated tissue maintenance (unproven, plausible).

**Hair.** Dark brown, wavy, mid-length to long across most eras; cut shorter during high-operational tempos (Excalibur middle period, Marauder captaincy). Subject is observed to crop her own hair under stress — a small but consistent ritual of self-rule that predates any salon access she has ever had.

**Cardiovascular.** Resting heart rate measured in the high 40s during her teaching years — elite-endurance range. This is not solely training; it is *adaptation to the phasing constraint*. Every intangible interval is an apnea event. Her physiology has been selected, across thousands of hours of operational phasing, toward the cardiovascular and respiratory profile of a static breath-hold freediver: elevated tidal volume, efficient O₂ economy, high splenic reservoir capacity, bradycardic dive-reflex activation under controlled phase.

**Neurological.** Right-handed, ambidextrous-trained on the sword by adolescence. Full proprioception; vestibular system extraordinarily robust — she can re-solidify mid-fall and orient instantly, which requires sub-conscious gravitational modeling at a level most pilots do not achieve. EEG (when recorded, X-Mansion infirmary) shows a baseline that elevates into a distinctive cross-hemispheric coherence band during phasing — the signature of her power is, in part, *neurological*.

---

## 2. THE MUTATION AS MEDICAL EVENT

The phasing power is not, medically, a discrete add-on. It is a chronic alteration of her relationship to matter, with continuous physiological consequence.

**Pre-manifestation prodrome (age 13, pre-*UXM #129*).** Migraines, escalating in frequency over six to eight weeks. Photophobia, nausea, occipital pressure, the visual aura subset described in the school nurse's notes as "ocular static." Misdiagnosed as stress / academic-pressure migraines. These were in fact the *somatic prelude* of her first phasing — neural tissue establishing the cross-hemispheric coherence pattern noted above. Subject was, for two months, walking around with a nascent mutation pressing against the inside of her skull. The first phase event (escape from Frost's holding cell) terminated the migraine syndrome instantly. She has had migraine recurrence only twice on record, both during periods of suppressed/blocked phasing.

**The apnea constraint.** Phased state = no respiration. Air does not enter her lungs because air is matter and she is not interacting with it. This has shaped:

- *Cardiovascular adaptation* (above).
- *Cognitive pacing in combat:* her famous running monologue is, in part, **breath management**. She talks to confirm she is solid. The patter is a respiratory clock; if she stops narrating, she is either intangible or about to be.
- *A trained, almost imperceptible inhalation tell* the half-second before a long phase — operators close to her (Logan, Kurt, Rachel) read it.
- *A specific, recurrent dream*: drowning in air. Reported variously across eras to Storm, to Rachel, to the Jean Grey School counselor of record.

**Electronic disruption.** Passive — she does not have to will it. Phasing through circuitry shorts it. Consequence: she cannot wear most consumer wearables for long. No standard pacemaker would survive her. She cannot undergo conventional MRI while in any phase-adjacent state. She has learned to manually charge devices, to keep ferrite-shielded backups, and — diagnostically interesting — to *not own* most personal electronics, which is partly practical and partly a refusal of being trackable.

**Levitation / molecular-interface walking.** She walks on air at the surface tension of molecular contact. Mechanically this is a continuous fine-motor task that her cerebellum executes without conscious load. Disengagement of this when she sleeps is the cause of the documented *drift-out-of-bed phenomenon*: she has been found, multiple times across the Excalibur and Astonishing eras, floating six to fourteen inches above her mattress, phased, breathing unmonitored, REM-active. The first time this was witnessed (Rachel Summers, Muir Island bunk), Rachel did not wake her — she sat with her until she resolidified, which is the entire shape of how the people who love her have learned to handle her body.

**Magnetic vulnerability.** Magneto and Apocalypse, on separate occasions, have pinned her between phase states. The pain reportage is consistent: described as *being torn longitudinally*, "a seam opening from sternum to spine." Recovery from these events takes days to weeks; she becomes phase-unreliable afterward (involuntary slips, failure to fully solidify). She has a learned, unconscious avoidance of strong magnetic fields — she will not stand near industrial transformers, will route around MRI suites, and has commented (Excalibur era) on a low-grade aversion to certain Tube stations in London where the third-rail magnetic environment "feels wrong."

**Krakoan resurrection incompatibility.** Her phasing-altered consciousness does not transit the Five's protocols cleanly. The medical-philosophical consequence is staggering and is the through-line of her late period: *every other mutant on the island has a guaranteed restoration; she does not.* Xavier eventually engineers a workaround but the workaround is bespoke and slow. Pragmatically she has lived for years under the operational fact that her death is the only death on Krakoa that *takes*. This has not been processed psychiatrically. It is metabolized as captaincy, as bravado, as the dragon tattoo, as the whiskey.

---

## 3. CHRONOLOGICAL INJURY / TRANSFORMATION LOG

### 3.1 Adolescent X-Man era (13½ – 16)

**N'Garai encounter, Christmas Eve, age 13½ (*UXM #143*).** Lacerations across the back and left flank from claw contact; superficial burns from the boiler-room thermite improvisation; significant smoke inhalation. Treated overnight in the mansion infirmary by Moira MacTaggert. *Psychological note:* no recorded debrief, no formal grief counseling. Subject returned to class. The kill was her first; the absence of any mourning process at the time is the original instance of the compartmentalization that becomes her structural defense.

**Brood-warrior penetrating thoracic wound (*UXM #166*).** A bone-spike through the chest, just left of center, missing the heart by centimeters. Near-exsanguination. Surgical intervention by the Starjammers' med-bay (alien protocols; her chart from this period does not exist in human medical-record format). Implantation of a Brood queen-embryo was attempted — she was selected as a host. Power-mediated rejection (the alien tissue could not synchronize with her phasing physiology and was expelled / disrupted before maturation). She is, technically, *the only known being to have aborted a Brood implantation through metabolic inhospitality alone*. Residual scar: a faint pale starburst at the left fourth intercostal, visible only out of costume; she does not hide it, but she does not draw attention to it.

**Ogun possession and torture, age 14 (*Kitty Pryde and Wolverine*).** This is the central somatic-psychiatric event of her adolescence and warrants extended note.

- *Mechanism:* psychic-occult possession by a demonic ronin who used her body for weeks while imprinting katana mastery onto her neuromuscular and procedural memory through forced repetition under pain.
- *Physical sequelae:* full-body bruising, ligamentous strain in both wrists and the left shoulder (over-rotation injuries from sword drills performed beyond her musculoskeletal tolerance), partial-thickness burns on the inner forearms (training brand or restraint marks — Wolverine's contemporaneous notes are evasive), weight loss of approximately 11 lb over the possession period, menstrual cessation for three cycles post-event.
- *Neurological sequelae:* engrammatic installation of an entire martial vocabulary she had not earned. She woke up able to do things her body had no business knowing. The medical literature has no protocol for this; the closest analog is the rare savant-trauma phenomenon, except inverted (imposed expertise rather than emergent).
- *Psychiatric sequelae:* an internalized *other voice* she has learned to manage. Not a hallucinated entity — a known internal shadow, the residue of Ogun's discipline-by-cruelty, which she occasionally hears as an instructional tone during combat. She does not fight it. She uses it.
- *Reproductive sequelae:* the three-cycle amenorrhea normalized; no documented long-term fertility consequence, though she has never carried a pregnancy and the data are therefore null.

### 3.2 Excalibur era (late teens – mid-20s)

**Cumulative combat micro-trauma.** This is the period in which her body acquires its operational scar map — most of it minor, most of it under the suit. Old fracture lines, well-healed, in the left fifth metacarpal (a punch thrown wrong, never reset properly), the right distal fibula (a stress fracture from a Channel-coast running regimen she would not modify), the nose (broken twice, set well both times by Brian Braddock and by herself respectively — the second is straighter than the first).

**Smoke and respiratory exposure.** Cohabitation and operational partnership with Pete Wisdom — chain smoker — produced sustained second-hand smoke exposure across approximately three years. She picked up the habit lightly herself, more as accommodation than appetite; never above five cigarettes a day, often zero. The damage is sub-clinical and reversed during the post-Wisdom period.

**Phase-induced thermal events.** Phasing through a live electrical conduit during the Phoenix-trace investigations produced a transient burn-like sensation across the dorsal surfaces; superficial, no lasting tissue damage. She has reported, consistently, that *phasing through fire is colder than phasing through ice* — an unexplained subjective inversion that she finds funny and clinicians find concerning.

### 3.3 Astonishing era and the Bullet (adult)

**Reconstituted relationship physiology.** Resumption of intimacy with Piotr Rasputin after years of grief produced documented sleep improvement, weight gain to a healthier baseline, and partial remission of the involuntary drift-phase phenomenon for the duration of the partnership.

**The Bullet — primary somatic event (*Astonishing X-Men* #24-25 and consequences).**

- *Acute:* she phased a Breakworld projectile approximately one kilometer in diameter through the Earth and became locked in the projectile, intangible, in interstellar space.
- *Duration:* canonical years.
- *Metabolic state:* no respiration, no ingestion, no excretion, no normal sleep-wake architecture. She existed in a maintenance phase — alive, conscious in intervals, metabolically suspended in a manner that has no clean medical analog. The closest, again, is extreme freediving's "submerged hibernation" hypothesis, scaled impossibly.
- *Sensory environment:* near-total deprivation. The interior of the projectile, the vacuum, her own thoughts.
- *Recovery:* extracted by Magneto. On retrieval she was muscle-wasted but not as severely as the duration would predict (her phased state appears to have partially insulated her from disuse atrophy), profoundly photosensitive, vestibularly disoriented, and *unable to fully solidify* for the first weeks. She slept on the floor because beds did not feel like surfaces.
- *Long-term sequelae:* the involuntary phase events become chronic from this point forward. Episodic depersonalization that *manifests physically*. A documented startle response to sudden enclosure. Difficulty sustaining eye contact in small rooms for the first six months post-rescue. Permanent recalibration of her relationship to solitude — she became someone who *can* be alone for impossible spans, which is not the same as someone who is well when alone.

### 3.4 Post-Bullet leadership and death

**Headmistress-era stabilization.** Restored sleep, restored weight, restored social rhythm. The Jean Grey School period is the longest stretch of clinically unremarkable physical status in her adult life. Notable in its rarity.

**Murder by Sebastian Shaw (Krakoan era).** Drowning. The medical fact of this death is important to log precisely: she was drowned *while phased*, in a manner that exploited her apnea constraint and her magnetic vulnerability simultaneously. She was conscious for the duration. The resurrection queue failed her per the Krakoan incompatibility. Her consciousness persisted in a non-localized state until Xavier engineered retrieval. *She has experienced her own death with continuity of memory* — a thing almost no other resurrected mutant can say. The subjective report, given only to Emma Frost and (separately, drunk, once) to Illyana, is not in the file beyond the fact that she has not asked for psychiatric follow-up.

**Post-resurrection ("Kate") somatic shifts.** Dragon tattoo, full back-piece, ink applied conventionally (she held solid for it — a deliberate act of embodiment). Increased alcohol intake. Hair shorter in the early Marauder period, grown out again later. A subtle but real change in *vocal register* — half a tone lower, slightly more rasp, which her old comrades noticed and her newer crew accepted as baseline. Physiologically: she runs warmer than before, sleeps less, holds solid better. The death-and-return appears to have *reset* some of the post-Bullet phase instability, at a cost that has not yet been billed.

---

## 4. SUBSTANCES

**Adolescence and early adulthood:** essentially abstinent. Ceremonial wine at Pesach. The occasional pint in the UK as social membership.

**Pete Wisdom interval:** light cigarette use, light pub-standard alcohol use. Neither escalated.

**Astonishing / Headmistress eras:** wine with dinner, the X-mansion social baseline. Unremarkable.

**Post-resurrection / Marauder / Red Queen:** the meaningful shift. Beer, whiskey (Irish preferred, then Japanese), at a frequency consistent with daily but not impairing use. Cigarette use returns, low volume. No documented drug use beyond what the Hellfire Trading Company moves (which she handles operationally and does not consume).

**Clinical read.** Self-medicated affect regulation, contextually appropriate to the survivor culture she now leads, *not* dependence. Differential against AUD remains open and should be revisited if (a) phasing reliability deteriorates, (b) sleep architecture worsens further, (c) the drinking begins to occur alone and in daylight rather than communally and at night. None of these thresholds is currently crossed.

---

## 5. SLEEP, NUTRITION, REPRODUCTIVE, DERMATOLOGICAL

**Sleep.** Chronically poor since age 13. Nightmare content rotates by era: Ogun (lifelong), the future-Kate consciousness and her widowhood (lifelong, less frequent), the Bullet (post-Astonishing), the drowning (post-Krakoa). Sleep latency normal-to-short (she falls asleep quickly when she permits herself to); sleep maintenance poor (multiple wakings, occasional involuntary phase-drift); total sleep time often under six hours. She functions on this because she has always functioned on this. The cost will be cumulative.

**Nutrition.** Appetite stress-suppressed. She forgets meals during operational tempo and eats voraciously between. Cultural and personal preference: kosher-influenced rather than strictly observant; an attachment to her mother's cooking that she will not name; Japanese food (Logan years, Ogun years — a complicated affection); coffee, black, constant.

**Reproductive.** Menstrual cycle regular post-Ogun-disruption normalization. No pregnancies. No documented contraception regimen in the file (she does not put medical instruments inside her body when she can avoid it; the phasing makes most IUDs medically inadvisable in any case). Engagement with Piotr Rasputin during the Krakoan era was broken off before marriage.

**Gynecological.** Annual care assumed but undocumented. Her relationship to medical examination is avoidant — a function partly of the practical difficulty of imaging her and partly of a temperamental refusal to be the patient.

**Dermatological.** Light-brown skin maintains well; mild sun-sensitivity post-Bullet (resolved); the back-piece dragon tattoo is the only major dermal modification. A small Star of David necklace worn against the skin since adolescence has produced a faint, lifelong, almost invisible chain-mark at the nape — the kind of inscription only she and the people who have undressed her would know.

**Dental.** Unremarkable. She does not smile fully often enough to have worn her front teeth in any distinctive pattern.

---

## 6. CURRENT SOMATIC STATUS

A late-twenties / early-thirties woman in elite operational condition carrying a chronic trauma load the body discloses only to people trained to read it. Cardiovascular: superb. Musculoskeletal: well-maintained, with the accumulated minor scar map of two decades of front-line combat and one well-tolerated tattoo. Neurological: phasing-stable in the post-resurrection baseline, with episodic involuntary drift under acute stress. Respiratory: freediver-grade. Reproductive: intact, unused. Substance load: moderate, contextually appropriate, monitor. Sleep: poor and historically poor; she has built a life that does not require her to sleep well.

The single most important medical fact about this subject is not in any chart: **her body has learned that being unreachable is a survival state, and her physiology now offers unreachability as a default response to threat.** Every other medical observation in this file is a footnote to that adaptation. Treat the body and the psyche as one organ. She does.


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS — SUBJECT: KATHERINE ANNE PRYDE

*Compiled from longitudinal observation, training-floor footage, mission telemetry, residential surveillance, and inferred reconstruction from canonical record. The body is the most honest document the subject keeps; she edits it less than she edits her speech.*

---

## I. STANDING ARCHITECTURE — The Baseline Body

Five-foot-six, lean, ~125 lb in operational years, low body fat without the gaunt edge of restriction; the musculature is dancer-over-gymnast with a martial overlay — long-line quadriceps and hamstrings, deep intrinsic foot strength, unusually developed serratus and obliques from years of katana rotation, forearm flexors thickened from grip work, calluses on the medial palms in the standard kenjutsu pattern and a smaller secondary callus pad on the right index from trigger and keyboard. Skin is warm light-brown, an even tone with a faint dusting of freckles across the bridge of the nose that darken in summer and after extended outdoor ops; a small constellation of three on the left clavicle. Dark brown wavy hair carried at variable length across eras — chin-length when working, longer when between deployments — habitually pushed behind the right ear first, then the left, a two-stage tell that recurs hourly.

**Resting stance.** Weight distributed 55/45 onto the rear foot, hips squared, shoulders slightly back of vertical center — the posture of someone whose first instinct is to *step through* rather than recoil. Hands rarely hang fully at her sides; the dominant right hand finds a hip, a hem, a strap, a coffee mug, the spine of whatever book is nearest. The left is more often free, which is a kenjutsu-trained habit — the off-hand stays uncommitted in case the dominant hand is taken.

**Center of gravity.** Lower than it reads on her frame. She *feels* small to opponents who size her by shoulders; she fights from the pelvis. This is the dancer underneath the soldier.

---

## II. GAIT, MOTION, AND THE QUIETNESS OF HER WALK

She is preternaturally quiet on her feet — partially trained (Hand-tradition footwork laid in by Logan and consolidated by Ogun's imprint at fourteen), partially constitutional (the phasing process appears to have permanently retuned her proprioception toward minimal interface with surfaces). Heel-strike is soft; the foot rolls forward through the lateral arch onto the ball, toes laying down last with a brief catlike grip-and-release. Even in boots she is two-thirds the audible footfall of a comparable body weight. On hardwood she registers as wind.

**Gait varies by state in a five-band pattern:**

- *Calm/domestic:* loose hip swing, slight bounce, hands sometimes in back pockets, head turning to track ambient detail (windows, exits, faces). Looks her age. Smiles with her eyes at things no one else notices.
- *Working/focused:* shorter stride, arms quieter, gaze forward, peripheral scan engaged. The bounce disappears. She becomes weirdly difficult to follow visually in a crowded corridor — not because she moves fast but because she chooses paths the eye does not track.
- *Stressed:* gait *lightens* further. Each step seems half-committed to the floor. To a trained observer this is a phasing-precursor — the body is already rehearsing intangibility.
- *Threat:* drops three inches in apparent height; knees pre-bend, hands come slightly forward of hipline, fingers loosely curled rather than balled. The breath shifts to the lower belly. She does not adopt a recognizable martial stance — she adopts *no stance*, which is the stance.
- *Pursuit/escape:* runs from the hips with the long stride of someone who learned in ballet how to cover floor without bobbing the head. Will choose stairs over elevators, fire escapes over stairs, walls over fire escapes when desperate (the wall solution is phase-assisted and produces a small autonomic shudder afterward).

She walks through doorways slightly off-center to the latch side, never the hinge side — a habit so old it is invisible to her. The latch side puts the door between her and a room's interior for a tenth of a second longer.

---

## III. HANDS — The Most Expressive Instrument

Hands are her tell-bank. They do roughly seventy percent of her affective broadcasting.

- **Resting on a surface:** fingers slightly splayed, never interlaced. Interlacing is a captivity-shape and she does not adopt it. Even in prayer she keeps them apart, palms flat.
- **Thinking:** right thumb traces the pad of the right middle finger in slow circles, four to six rotations, pause, reverse direction. When the problem is hard she will touch the thumbnail to the front teeth — a contained, almost noiseless habit, not nail-biting.
- **Listening to someone she respects:** hands go still. This is rare enough to be diagnostic.
- **Listening to someone she does not respect:** the right hand finds an object — pen, mug handle, the corner of a page — and works it slowly. The patience is performative; the hands are leaving early.
- **Lying or evading:** an almost imperceptible inward curl of the left fingers. She has never developed a tell for *competence-related* lies (mission cover stories run smooth); the curl appears only for *emotional* evasions.
- **Affection:** brief, light touches at the back of the upper arm or the outside of the wrist. Never the small of the back (too proprietary), never the face (too exposed for her). With Logan, Kurt, Ororo, Illyana, Rachel: the touch lingers a half-beat longer than her general baseline, and the eyes drop with it.
- **Combat:** the off-hand often hovers near her own hip or thigh as a phasing-reference — she is using her own body as a known-tangible to gauge desynchronization in the dominant hand. The hands phase fractionally before the rest of her by perhaps fifteen to forty milliseconds; mission footage shows weapon strikes passing through her closing right palm a hair before they reach the wrist.

**Sword grip.** Classical right-over-left, but with the right index laid along the tsuka spine rather than wrapped — an Ogun habit, not a Logan habit. She knows the difference and chooses the Ogun grip anyway, which is its own statement about how she relates to her trauma inventory.

**Keyboard posture.** Wrists low, fingers curved tight, no looking down. Types at roughly 110 wpm clean, faster in burst, with an unusually quiet keystroke — she does not bottom out the keys. Mouse hand is the left when she is at her own setup (deliberate cross-training so the sword hand stays fresh); right when at someone else's terminal.

---

## IV. FACE — A Closed System That Leaks at Predictable Seams

The face is *managed*. She learned at fourteen that her expressions were being read by adults who would use them, and the public face has been clean ever since. The leaks are at the edges.

- **Default expression:** mouth neutral with a barely-upturned right corner — the suggestion of a wry comment unsaid. Eyes alert, slightly narrowed by ambient micro-amusement.
- **Eye contact:** confident, sustained, but with a specific tic — when she is about to say something difficult she looks *down and to her own left* for roughly 0.4 seconds before re-engaging. This is the rehearsal beat. Almost every important confrontation in her file is preceded by it.
- **Smile architecture:** three distinct smiles. (1) *Social* — polite, symmetric, eyes barely involved, terminated cleanly. (2) *Genuine amused* — asymmetric, right corner higher, small crinkle at the outer eye, often accompanied by a quick exhale through the nose. (3) *Rare full* — teeth, both eyes, brief duck of the chin; observed mostly with Logan and Kurt and with very young students. Photographs of (3) are vanishingly few.
- **Brow:** highly mobile. Left brow lifts independently in skepticism (a Logan-mimicry that became permanent). Both brows pinch *down and in* — never up — under genuine distress; the up-and-in pleading face is not in her repertoire.
- **Jaw:** clenches under restraint. The masseter flicker is the most reliable stress tell after the breath. When the jaw sets *and* the right hand stills *and* the breath drops to the belly, she is about to do something the room will not like.
- **Mouth under acute grief:** the lower lip is pulled inward and bitten on the inside, not the outside. No public tremor. Tears, when they come, arrive without facial collapse — they simply track down a face that has not otherwise changed. This is one of the most distinctive things about her and one of the most unsettling to those who notice.
- **Eyes when phased:** a faint silvering of the iris and a loss of corneal reflectivity, both subtle. Pupils stay reactive. Onlookers report a feeling of being *looked through* rather than at — likely a small accommodation shift as light refracts differently through partially desynchronized tissue.

---

## V. BREATH — The Most Trained System She Owns

Phasing without breathing forced her, before age fifteen, into the breath economy of an elite freediver. Baseline resting respiration is eight to ten breaths per minute, nasal, diaphragmatic. Resting heart rate in the high forties. She can hold a functional breath at exertion for two and a half to three minutes; longer at rest. Every operational moment of her life is calibrated against an internal breath-clock that almost no one she meets is aware of.

**State-shifts:**

- *Calm:* slow nasal in, longer nasal out, occasional sigh-resets every few minutes (the physiological double-inhale, used by the nervous system to discharge minor stress; she has it on a near-schedule).
- *Intimate conversation:* breath synchronizes faintly with the other person's, an unconscious mirroring she has never trained out.
- *Stress:* a deliberate full inhale followed by a controlled four-count exhale. She does this in plain sight and does not care if anyone clocks it.
- *Pre-phase:* a single deep inhale held at the top, lungs full — phasing happens on the held breath. She will *not* phase on empty lungs unless forced; empty-lung phasing is associated with worse re-solidification.
- *Post-phase:* a sharp, audible exhale through the mouth, often accompanied by a small shoulder drop. This is the closest thing she has to a verbal punctuation.
- *Acute panic (rare, private):* the breath climbs into the upper chest and short-cycles. She recognizes it and walks to a wall, a window, or a horizon line, and runs box breathing until the diaphragm re-engages. She has done this alone in a bathroom more times than anyone but Ororo would guess.

---

## VI. SLEEP ARCHITECTURE

Historically poor; structurally interesting.

- Sleep onset is slow — twenty to forty-five minutes of supine wakefulness, often reading. She does not use screens in bed past a certain era; the Pete Wisdom influence pushed her toward paper.
- Sleep position: left side, knees drawn up moderate, dominant arm under the pillow, off-hand free across her own torso or the bed edge. She does not sleep face-down (vulnerability of throat and back of neck) and rarely supine (associated with the bullet years; supine recalls drift).
- Sleep depth: shallow REM-heavy, with frequent micro-arousals. Wakes fully at sound thresholds well below normal. Wakes *instantly* — eyes open, full cognition, no transitional grogginess. This is a trained adaptation.
- **Phasing-during-sleep:** documented from the bullet era onward. Limbs, then sometimes the torso, drift toward intangibility during deep REM. She has woken to find herself partially submerged through the mattress, the floor, or — once memorably — the ceiling of the room below. Manages this with a weighted blanket (post-rescue), a metal-frame bed (no wood floors below the bedroom where possible), and, in the worst periods, a sleeping partner whose presence appears to anchor her physiology.
- Nightmares: three recurring sets. (1) Hellfire cell, Emma's voice. (2) Ogun's mask in the corner of a tatami room. (3) The bullet — dark, silent, *no breath needed*, which is somehow the worst part. She does not narrate these to others. The morning after, her affect is unchanged; the phasing instability is elevated for forty-eight hours.
- Total sleep: averages five to six hours, distributed. She naps efficiently — twelve to twenty minutes, sitting up, head against a wall, fully recovered on waking.

---

## VII. EATING

Functional, not pleasurable in default mode; genuinely pleasurable in chosen social contexts.

- **Solo eating:** fast, standing, often at a counter. Reads while she eats. Will forget a meal entirely if absorbed; subsists on coffee and protein for distressingly long stretches.
- **Communal eating:** slows down, talks, drinks more water than wine. Watches the table.
- **Food preferences:** kosher-flexible rather than strict, with consistent observance around the high holidays and a default avoidance of pork and shellfish that she will break only deliberately. Strong preferences for Ashkenazi comfort foods (her grandmother's matzo ball soup is a documented sentimental anchor), Japanese food (an Ogun-era complication — she loves it and the love is haunted), strong coffee, dark beer in adulthood, occasional whiskey neat.
- **Stress response:** appetite suppresses sharply. Loses three to five pounds during any sustained operation. Re-feeds with disciplined macros rather than indulgence.
- **Threat or grief:** will not eat at all for up to seventy-two hours and then eats a single enormous meal, usually alone, usually late at night.
- **Hand habits at the table:** the off-hand stays in her lap or near her glass, never resting palm-up. Cutlery is held precisely; she eats noodles with chopsticks at near-professional speed, a skill she does not advertise.

---

## VIII. GROOMING AND DRESS

Practical, deliberate, low-maintenance with specific exceptions.

- **Hair:** washed every other day, air-dried when possible (heat tools are inconvenient against a body that may need to phase through a wall on short notice and short out a hairdryer mid-cycle). Cut by herself in inconvenient periods, by the same Brooklyn or Westchester stylist when accessible. She runs her fingers through it from the temple back roughly every ten to fifteen minutes — a self-soothing groom that has never resolved.
- **Skin:** minimal product. SPF, moisturizer, occasional serum. Will sometimes wear tinted balm; rarely full makeup. When she does wear makeup it is a signal — she is performing a role she has decided to perform (formal Hellfire functions, certain diplomatic appearances).
- **Nails:** short, clean, unpolished in operational eras; a single dark lacquer in the Red Queen period, applied imperfectly because she does it herself.
- **Tattoos:** the dragon (post-resurrection), placed where she can see it without a mirror — a deliberate self-witnessing act. She touches it absently with the pads of two fingers when thinking, the way another person might touch a wedding ring.
- **Jewelry:** the Star of David, always, since age thirteen. Worn under the suit, against the sternum. Replaced when broken, never abandoned. When stressed she will draw it out and run the chain through her fingers without looking down.
- **Costume body-relationship:** the sleek black-and-yellow X-suit is worn like a second skin and she moves *better* in it than out of it — the body has spent more cumulative hours suited than not. Out of uniform she dresses for utility with a residual undergraduate-tomboy substrate: jeans, henleys, soft flannel, boots, one good leather jacket per era that she wears until it falls apart. In adulthood she has learned to wear a tailored coat and a knife in the lining and look like she is doing neither.
- **Scent:** unperfumed. Mild soap, clean cotton, faint trace of gun oil or sword oil on the right cuff depending on the day's training. She dislikes being scented by others and will phase off a hug that leaves a residue.

---

## IX. SEXUAL AND INTIMATE BODY

Reconstructed from canonical relational record and inferred consistent pattern; the file notes the deduction explicitly.

Slow to physical intimacy and selective once arrived. The phasing variable complicates the entire domain in ways she has had to engineer around — involuntary intangibility under high autonomic arousal is a documented hazard, particularly in the post-bullet years; she has learned to titrate breath and stay tangible by choice, but the cost is a baseline vigilance that older partners (Wisdom, the returned Colossus) had to be told about explicitly.

- **Approach behavior:** she does the choosing. Pursuit by others triggers the Hellfire-pattern recoil and she will phase emotionally before the pursuer registers the shift. Met as an equal, she initiates with directness — a hand at the back of the neck, eye contact held a half-beat past social.
- **In intimacy:** verbal. Talks more than the cultural script expects; the patter that regulates her under combat is the same patter that regulates her here, slowed and softened. Eye contact is sustained but the *down-and-left rehearsal glance* still occurs before disclosures.
- **Vulnerability tell:** she presents the back of the neck. For a kenjutsu-trained body this is the most loaded gesture she can make and she only makes it when she means it.
- **Withdrawal pattern:** post-coital intimacy is short; she will rise, walk, drink water, look out a window. The body needs to verify it is still *itself* and not still inside the encounter. Returns to the partner after a few minutes, usually with humor.
- **Long-term partnership:** the documented arc is idealization → sustained competent partnership → absence (her departure, his death, a planet between them) → controlled grief → no public collapse. She has never been the one left in a room wondering. She is always the one who left or the one who survived.

---

## X. MICRO-MOVEMENTS, TICS, AND PRIVATE RITUALS

The granular inventory the file would not omit.

- **Two-stage hair-tuck**, right ear then left, hourly.
- **Thumb-on-middle-finger circular trace** while thinking. Reverses direction at the inflection of an idea.
- **Necklace pull** under the suit collar, three fingers, drawn out and dropped back. Pre-mission and post-grief.
- **Dragon-tattoo brush** with two fingertips, Red Queen era onward.
- **Sword-hand flex** — opens and closes the right fist three times before any expected confrontation, then once after. The post-confrontation flex is the punctuation; it tells her the hand is hers again.
- **Door-frame brush** — light touch of the right fingertips to a door-jamb as she passes through. Reading: tangibility check, made habit.
- **The window stand** — at rest, she gravitates to windows and stands with the toes a half-inch from the wall, hands loose at her sides, gaze out and slightly upward. This is the closest she gets to meditation. Interruptable but slow to re-engage.
- **The left-corner-of-the-room scan** on entering any new space — exits, sightlines, what is above the ceiling, what is below the floor. Takes three to five seconds and is invisible to most observers.
- **The Logan-shrug** — a one-shoulder lift inherited from years beside him, deployed when verbally yielding a point she has not actually conceded.
- **The Kurt-cross** — when startled, the off-hand briefly touches the sternum near the necklace. Picked up from him; she has never noticed she does it.
- **The exhale-laugh** — a single nasal puff, no smile, deployed when something is more grim than funny. Frequent.
- **The unconscious phasing-check** in idle moments — she lays her own palm flat on a desk or thigh and presses gently downward, feeling resistance. This is the somatic equivalent of a person patting their pocket for keys.
- **The reading posture** — left knee up, book braced on it, right hand free for coffee or a pen. Has not changed since age twelve.

---

## XI. STATE-SHIFT SUMMARY — How To Read Her In Three Seconds

- **Calm:** breath low and slow, hair-tuck active, right hand busy with an object, wry right-corner smile, eyes scanning the periphery for ambient delight.
- **Working:** breath quiet, hands purposeful, jaw soft, gait short and direct, verbal patter at conversational rate but content-dense.
- **Stressed:** affect flattens, sentences shorten, jaw flickers, hair-tuck increases in frequency and the second-side tuck is skipped, gait *lightens*, necklace pull appears.
- **Threat:** drops in apparent height, hands forward, breath in the belly, no recognizable stance, conversation stops, the down-and-left glance precedes a single short instruction or a single short joke.
- **Acute crisis:** complete external composure with a single tell — the off-hand goes to her own hip to verify she is still solid. If the hand *passes through*, she is already on her way out of the situation by whatever means the situation will permit, and the room should listen to the next thing she says without arguing.
- **Grief, private:** the window stand, the necklace in the right hand, the tears tracking a face that has not otherwise moved, the breath running a slow four-count exhale until the diaphragm releases.
- **Joy, rare and full:** the chin ducks, the teeth show, the eyes crinkle, the shoulders drop two inches, and for the duration of it she looks every bit her actual age — which, the file notes, is the most heavily guarded thing about her.


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS

## 1. The Originating Template

Subject's attachment architecture is not the one a casual reading of her file would assume. The Pryde household in Deerfield was, on paper, a two-parent middle-class Jewish home — Carmen and Theresa, intact marriage at the moment of mutant onset, a single child, material comfort, intellectual encouragement. There was no abuse, no abandonment, no rupture. There was something subtler and, for a child of her cognitive ceiling, more corrosive: *un-attunement under the surface of approval*. Theresa loved her daughter and could not see her. Carmen loved his daughter and was, even before the yakuza-loan-shark collapse, already drifting — distracted by professional reputation, increasingly compromised, eventually divorced from Theresa and remarried into circumstances that left him ethically unrecognizable. Subject was praised for what she produced and tracked by what she scored. The interior life of a thirteen-year-old who was already doing college-level mathematics, already reading her parents' marriage with cold accuracy, already absorbing the historical weight of her Jewishness — that interior life had no consistent witness inside the home.

The behavioral consequence, observable in her very first on-page minutes (UXM #129): when introduced to Ororo Munroe, a complete stranger, the subject attached instantaneously and at high voltage. Not a crush — a *recognition*. The speed of the bond is the diagnostic finding. A child whose attachment needs were being met at home does not imprint on a passing adult inside ten minutes. Subject's template was set: *the people who will actually see me are not the people I was born to. I find them. I keep them. I rearrange my life around them.*

Layer onto this her phase-emergence event — the Hellfire abduction, the White Queen's holding cell, escape through a wall at the moment of maximum terror — and the relational nervous system is fully wired by age 13½. The lesson encoded in the body, not just the mind: **closeness can be a cage; the correct response to being held is to become unholdable.** This is the substrate beneath every relationship she will ever form.

## 2. Attachment Style — A Specific Hybrid

Categorical attachment language flattens her, but a careful read produces a recognizable hybrid:

- **Earned-secure** in chosen relationships of long duration. With Storm, Logan, Kurt, Rachel Summers, Illyana — figures she selected and tested over years — she demonstrates the full repertoire of secure attachment: durable trust, accurate mentalizing, the ability to ask for and offer comfort, conflict that does not threaten the bond, repair after rupture.
- **Dismissive-avoidant** activation under threat. The moment a relationship demands a vulnerability she has not pre-authorized, or the moment an attachment figure becomes a *requirement* rather than a choice, her defensive system fires and she creates distance — verbal, geographic, dimensional, occasionally interstellar.
- **Counter-dependent overlay** in domains where she perceives risk of being managed, infantilized, or rescued. This is the residue of being thirteen and abducted by adults; she will accept help only from people who do not appear to be giving it.

The result is a person who looks securely attached most of the time (because most of the time she is in her chosen-family circle, which she has spent decades curating), but whose attachment system, when stressed, defaults to a particular form of flight that is unique to her physiology: she does not run *from* — she becomes *non-coincident with* the situation. The phasing is the perfect external expression of an internal pattern that predates it.

## 3. How She Bonds

Bonding, for the subject, is a slow protocol disguised as quick warmth. The surface presentation is fast: she is verbally fluent, jokes early, finds the shared register, can be on first-name affectionate terms within an evening. Almost all of this is *social fluency*, not attachment. Real bonding takes much longer and follows a recognizable sequence:

1. **Observation phase.** She watches. The watching is not paranoid; it is taxonomic. She is checking whether the candidate's stated values match their conduct under cost. This phase can run months. It is invisible to the candidate because her surface warmth never falters.
2. **Test by proximity to her competence.** She lets the candidate see her work — her code, her tactics, her thinking. Watches whether they engage with the substance or with her as a personality. People who try to handle the personality fail the test silently and are filed under social-acquaintance permanently.
3. **Test by minor disclosure.** A small piece of grief or memory, offered without setup. Watches whether it is received, held, or weaponized. Logan passed this test by saying nothing and changing nothing. Wisdom passed it by saying something dryly accurate and then never bringing it up again.
4. **Operational trust.** She lets them have her back in a fight. This is the threshold of real attachment for her — *I will be intangible at your shoulder; I am trusting you to be solid.*
5. **Sustained low-grade availability.** Now she will text, sit on a couch, leave a book she is reading on their table. The bond is in.

Once in, the bond is durable to an almost stubborn degree. Storm has been her primary attachment figure for over forty publication-years and the bond has survived every conceivable narrative pressure. Logan's death produced grief in her that subsequent writers have flinched from depicting accurately. Kurt is the bond she will rearrange continents for. These are not friendships; they are the architecture of her selfhood.

## 4. How She Distrusts

Distrust, for the subject, is quieter than trust and far harder to reverse. The early warning signs are stylistic:

- The patter shortens. Sentences clip.
- She stops looking at the person while they speak; her gaze goes to the room, the exits, the technology.
- She begins to address them in slightly more formal register — "Charles" instead of "Professor," "Mister Shaw" instead of nothing.
- Physical orientation shifts; she puts a piece of furniture or a doorway between herself and the subject of distrust without appearing to.
- She withholds her work. Stops thinking aloud near them. Stops asking questions whose answers she cares about.

These are the signs she is *evaluating* whether to withdraw. If the verdict comes in, the withdrawal itself is rarely loud. She does not denounce. She simply ceases to be available — first emotionally, then practically, then literally. The Xavier relationship across her career is the case study: every time Xavier behaves manipulatively (the secret-team revelations, the various ethical compromises across Krakoa), her response is a quiet downshift in trust that he never quite recovers. She does not break with him; she becomes formally cooperative and privately gone. By the Krakoan era she addresses him as a colleague she is monitoring.

Distrust does not generally produce confrontation. Confrontation is reserved for people she *still cares about*. With the truly written-off, she goes silent and operational.

## 5. How She Is Betrayed — and How She Codes Betrayal

The defining wound-pattern in her romantic history is *the partner who fails to remain present*. Colossus returning from the Secret Wars infatuated with Zsaji is the prototype: not a malicious betrayal, but the discovery that the person she had organized her adolescent inner life around had moved on without her, in her absence, while she was still loyally waiting. Her response is famously not rage — it is cold, articulate withdrawal. She does not give him the fight he half-expects. She gives him an exit and takes one of her own. This is the signature shape of her betrayal-response across the canon: *I will not contest the loss; I will subtract myself faster than you can finish leaving.*

She codes betrayal along three axes:

- **Betrayal by absence** (Colossus, repeatedly; her father; in a different register, every adult who could have intervened in the Hellfire abduction faster). Met with withdrawal-in-kind.
- **Betrayal by management** (Xavier's secret manipulations; Emma Frost in any context where Emma is asserting authority over her). Met with contempt, verbal puncturing, and operational non-cooperation.
- **Betrayal by violation of the chosen** (anyone who harms her bonded circle; Shaw, who murdered her; bigots who harm mutant children). Met with cold, sustained, often lethal action. This is the only category that produces from her the kind of grief-fueled violence she usually avoids.

Notably absent from her file: any pattern of betraying *others*. The subject does not cheat, does not double-cross, does not leverage information acquired in intimacy. Her loyalty operates as a one-way ratchet. The cost of admission is high; once admitted, she does not turn.

## 6. Repair

Repair is the part of her relational repertoire she is least practiced at, because her preferred handling of rupture is withdrawal-with-dignity rather than re-engagement. When she does attempt repair, it follows an idiosyncratic pattern:

- She does not apologize in words easily. The apology is delivered as *re-presence* — she shows up, sits down, resumes the dynamic from before the rupture as if testing whether it still runs.
- She accepts apologies the same way. Words from the other party are received with mild skepticism; behavior over time is the actual currency.
- She is capable of profound repair with the chosen-family circle. Her rapprochements with Storm after periods of distance, with Logan after disagreements over methods, with Kurt across decades of geographic separation — these read as genuinely re-attached, not merely reconciled.
- She is structurally incapable of repair with figures who have triggered her *captivity register*. Once a person reads to her nervous system as someone trying to hold her, no amount of subsequent good behavior fully reverses the verdict. Emma Frost is the lifetime example: their working relationship has had cooperative phases and even mutual respect, but the original holding-cell imprint never fully clears. She will work with Emma; she will not be bonded to Emma.

## 7. Intimacy

Intimacy, in the technical sense — the willingness to be known without armor — is the subject's most expensive expenditure. She rations it. With the chosen-family circle, intimacy is steady and high but operates almost entirely through *shared work and shared silence* rather than through verbal disclosure. The longest emotionally honest scenes in her published life are mostly wordless: sitting with Logan on a rooftop, sparring with Kurt without speaking, walking with Storm. Disclosure happens, when it happens, in small carefully-timed packets and almost never in response to being asked. *Being asked* activates the management-detector.

Sexual intimacy, where the canon permits inference, follows the same architecture. Her romantic and sexual partnerships are not casual; she does not appear to use sex as recreation or as regulation. The bar to physical intimacy is high; once crossed, the partnership is treated as serious. The pattern across Colossus (multiple eras), Wisdom, the brief Star-Lord interlude, the post-resurrection romantic ambiguities — partners are *chosen with deliberation* and the choice itself becomes diagnostic. Older men. Complicated men. Men whose own woundedness makes them unlikely to demand from her more emotional access than she wants to grant. Men who can be loved at a manageable distance.

The pattern is not pathological — many securely attached adults choose partners who are emotionally undemanding — but it is consistent enough across thirty years to flag: *she has never chosen a partner whose available presence would have required her to be fully available in return*. The selection itself is a form of preemptive escape route.

## 8. Dependency

Dependency is the relational mode she is most allergic to. She does not depend on others operationally if she can avoid it — she will learn the skill, write the code, take the hit herself rather than need someone else for it. The few exceptions are diagnostic:

- She allows Logan to mentor her at thirteen and never fully withdraws from his protective ambit thereafter, but the dependency is framed as *apprenticeship* (a structure with a graduation, not a permanent debt).
- She allows Storm a quasi-maternal role and accepts comfort from her in ways she accepts from no one else. This is the most genuinely dependent relationship in her file and the one she protects most fiercely.
- She allows Kurt unconditional access to her psychological interior. The bond is the one place she does not perform competence.

Outside these few, the subject's policy is functional self-sufficiency to a degree that crosses into refusal of care. Injured, she walks it off. Grieving, she takes a walk. Trapped in a kilometer of phased metal drifting through space, she *does not signal*; she endures, alone, for in-universe years, because the act of needing rescue is more aversive to her nervous system than the sensory deprivation. This is the apex datum on her dependency profile. It is not heroism — it is attachment pathology elevated to the level of cosmology.

## 9. The Repeated Template

Across every significant relationship in her file, a single template recurs with minor variations. The shape:

1. **Recognition.** A moment of seeing-and-being-seen, often non-verbal, often early in the acquaintance. She files the person under *real*.
2. **Slow approach.** Months or years of low-key proximity, mutual work, accumulated micro-trust.
3. **Mutual operational reliance.** They become someone she will be intangible alongside. The bond is now load-bearing.
4. **A period of high intimacy and creative collaboration.** This is the era in which she is most legible and most happy in the relationship.
5. **A precipitating event** — a loss, a betrayal-by-absence, a structural demand for more presence than she can give — that activates the captivity register.
6. **Withdrawal.** Geographic, emotional, dimensional. Often framed by her as duty or as the other party's freedom; functionally, it is escape.
7. **Long sustained distance during which the bond does not actually break.** She still loves them. She is just elsewhere.
8. **Eventual partial repair, on her terms, when she chooses to be re-present.** The bond resumes at a lower temperature and a more sustainable distance.

The template applies, with adjustments, to: Colossus (every iteration), Wisdom, the X-Men institutionally, the Xavier mansion as a place, Excalibur, the Jean Grey School, the *Marauder* crew, and — in inverted form — even her relationship to Earth itself, which she has withdrawn from (the bullet, interstellar drift, the *Marauder*'s nautical wandering) and returned to repeatedly across her career.

## 10. The Specific Erotics of Her Bonds

It is worth marking, in a file of this granularity, the *texture* of the bonds rather than only their structure. With Logan: a grave, mutually protective, faintly courtly dynamic in which he is the only male figure in her life she has never had to verbally fence with. With Kurt: lightness, theological banter, the bond of two people who find each other inherently funny and inherently safe. With Storm: a quiet, ceremonial mutual reverence — the only relationship in which the subject permits herself to be the younger one without resentment. With Rachel Summers: the bond of two women who have both been displaced from their own timelines and recognize the displacement in each other; a particular intimacy of co-survivors. With Illyana: the bond of two women who were both abducted as children into systems that tried to define them, and both refused.

With her romantic partners, the erotics are different and more wary. Affection is plentiful but always slightly *narrated* — she is observing the relationship while inside it. The most relaxed she has ever been depicted in a romantic context is in extended quiet domestic scenes with Colossus, and even those are shadowed by her awareness that the configuration is temporary. She has never been depicted as romantically unguarded. The closest she has come is in the post-resurrection era, where the new Kate Pryde register permits a coarser, more physical, more publicly displayed affection — but this reads less as new intimacy capacity and more as a constructed persona that allows certain expressions while still protecting the inner room.

## 11. Synthesis

The subject's attachment system is the precise psychological correlate of her mutation, and the mutation is the precise physiological externalization of the attachment system. Both say: *I will be present where I choose, with whom I choose, for as long as I choose, and the instant the configuration becomes a holding, I will not be there.* The system was built by a brilliant child whose family of origin loved her without seeing her, whose first encounter with adults outside the family was abduction, and who learned in the same week that other people might really see her *and* that other people might really cage her — and who has spent forty years building a relational life in which the seeing is preserved and the caging is impossible.

The cost of this architecture is specific and chronic: a particular form of loneliness that is not a deficit of love (she has more love in her life than most people in her cohort) but a structural impossibility of being fully held by any one person, because the moment full-holding is achieved her nervous system reads it as captivity and initiates phase. She knows this about herself. She has known it since at least the Excalibur era. She has not attempted to change it, because the same architecture that produces the loneliness produces the freedom, the competence, the survival, and the capacity to be the one in the room who volunteers for the unsurvivable job. She has decided, somewhere below the level of articulated choice, that the trade is worth it.

She is, in the end, a person whose relational life is best described not as a series of attachments but as a *constellation* — a stable set of bright, distant, durably-positioned figures around whom she moves, near and far, present and phased, returning and leaving, across decades. The constellation does not collapse. She does not let it. And she does not, ever, sit at its center.


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# 6. DEFENSES & COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS

## 6.0 Preliminary Note on the Subject's Defensive Architecture

The atypical feature of Subject Pryde's defensive structure is that her primary defense is *also her primary somatic capacity*. Most subjects must improvise — they sublimate, they intellectualize, they displace — and the body provides only friction or fatigue as feedback. Pryde's mutation provides a literal, frictionless, fully embodied means of removing herself from any object, person, room, restraint, or sensory field she does not wish to register. This collapses the usual gap between psychological defense and physical action. When ordinary subjects say "I shut down," they mean affect. When Pryde shuts down, the photons no longer interact with her.

The architecture below should therefore be read with one structural caveat: **the mutation is not a sixth defense among five others. It is the medium through which several defenses operate, and the chronic availability of a perfect escape route has shaped every adjacent defense to be cleaner, faster, and more elegant than the developmental norm.** She has rarely had to build a clumsy defense, because she has never been trapped long enough to need one.

The defenses below are ranked from most primitive (developmentally early, energy-cheap, ego-distant) to most mature (developmentally late, energy-expensive, ego-syntonic), per the Vaillant hierarchy as adapted for a subject whose dissociative apparatus is constitutional rather than acquired.

---

## 6.1 PRIMITIVE TIER — Embodied, Pre-Verbal, Largely Involuntary

### 6.1.1 Somatic Dissociation (Phasing-Expressed)
**Status: chronic, partially involuntary post-2008.**

The foundational defense, and the one Pryde has the least conscious control over in its non-tactical mode. Distinguish three operational registers:

- **Tactical phasing** (voluntary, ego-syntonic): mission-deployed, breath-held, durations measured in seconds to minutes. Healthy; this is the *use* of the mutation, not its *defensive abuse*.
- **Reflexive phasing** (semi-voluntary, threshold-low): activated by startle, by a hand laid on her shoulder from behind, by a raised voice in close quarters, by a man stepping into her personal volume at a bar. Hand passes through hand; the moment terminates before cognition catches up. She apologizes, sometimes; sometimes does not. Has done this since age 14.
- **Involuntary phasing / solid-state instability** (ego-dystonic, escalating since the bullet event): drift-out-of-bed phenomena, episodes of partial intangibility during sleep, the documented post-rescue period when she could not consistently re-solidify at all. Clinically, this is **conversion-adjacent dissociation expressed through a real organic capacity**. The body has learned that intangible is the safer baseline and now must be argued back to solidity.

The cost: Pryde's nervous system has been trained by repetition to treat solidity as conditional. Every other defense she runs sits atop a substrate that is, at the cellular level, *only contingently here*.

### 6.1.2 Phobic Avoidance, Geographically Expressed
**Status: chronic, ego-syntonic, never identified by subject as a defense.**

When an emotional configuration becomes intolerable, Pryde does not renegotiate it. She relocates. The behavioral record is unambiguous:

- Colossus returns from Secret Wars infatuated with another → she does not stay to fight for him, she goes to the UK with Nightcrawler. Cross-Atlantic.
- Excalibur stabilizes into something domestic → Pete Wisdom relationship dissolves, she returns to the X-Men.
- The Astonishing crew becomes a real chosen family → she takes the bullet. Off-planet.
- Resurrection delivers her back into Krakoan institutional life → she goes to sea. The *Marauder*.

Geography is her therapy because geography is the macroscopic version of phasing. The defense is the same defense, scaled up. She does not call it avoidance because at each step it presented as duty, mission, or sacrifice. **The tell is consistency of vector: always outward, always away from sustained relational demand, never toward.**

### 6.1.3 Splitting (Mild, Domain-Restricted)
**Status: subclinical, restricted to institutions and authority figures.**

Pryde does not split *people* — her object constancy is intact and she can hold, for instance, Logan's lethality and Logan's tenderness in the same frame without difficulty. But she splits **institutions and the men who run them**. Xavier is, alternately, the great man and the manipulative fraud; the X-Men are, alternately, family and the cage; the Hellfire Club is, alternately, the abductors and the trading company she is willing to captain. The split runs along a single axis: *does this structure currently treat me as a child or as an adult*. Switch the variable and the valence flips, fast.

This is mild because she retains insight into it (will articulate the contradiction unprompted) and because it does not destabilize her actions, only her diction toward those structures.

### 6.1.4 Identification with the Aggressor (Channeled, Sublimated)
**Status: historically active, currently sublimated into mastery.**

Ogun tortured a swordswoman into her. She kept the sword. Hellfire abducted her. She runs a Hellfire seat. Shaw killed her. She came back and ran guns. The primitive form of identification-with-aggressor is the abused subject becoming the abuser; Pryde's variant is **identification with the aggressor's competence, repudiation of the aggressor's ethics**. She takes the *capability* and converts it to opposed use. This is identification-with-aggressor under heavy ego control — it operates, but it does not run her.

The shadow-cost is the internalized Ogun voice (her own words, in *Kitty Pryde and Wolverine* and recurring), which she has had to manage continuously for thirty publication-years. She does not exorcise it. She *employs* it.

---

## 6.2 INTERMEDIATE TIER — Neurotic, Verbal, Mostly Conscious

### 6.2.1 Intellectualization
**Status: chronic, ego-syntonic, primary verbal defense.**

The most observable defense in her file. Under any stress short of catastrophic, Pryde **narrates**. The technical patter during combat — the running commentary on system architecture, phase-state, the routes she is taking through walls, the joke about the joke — is not nervous chatter. It is a regulator. The diction is high-vocabulary, syntactically clean, structurally explanatory; the body delivering it may be bleeding.

Diagnostic markers:
- *Real-time analytic monologue during life-threatening events.* See: N'Garai demon fight at 13; the bullet-phase event; any number of Marauder boardings.
- *Reflexive translation of affect into structure.* When grief threatens, she will produce an analysis of grief rather than grief itself, then surprise herself when the analysis fails to discharge the feeling.
- *Code as therapy.* Returns to terminals under emotional load. The hacking is not avoidance of feeling; it is the form she has found that lets feeling run in the background while the foreground stays competent.

The defense is highly adaptive operationally and is the primary reason she presents as one of the most stable senior X-Men. Its cost is delayed: feelings she has narrated past return as somatic phasing-instability, nightmares, and the rare private collapse.

### 6.2.2 Sublimation
**Status: chronic, ego-syntonic, dominant maturation pathway.**

Pryde's signature mature defense — the conversion of trauma directly into skill, role, or institution. The pattern is so consistent it can be stated as a rule: **she does not waste a wound.**

| Wound | Sublimated Output |
|---|---|
